The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
(Published by Authority)
PART IV (B) — LOcAL  GOVERNmENT
Local Government Notifications
1a- pG 5995 - 07 (09/2022) 
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
Pradeshiya sabha - KuliyaPitiya
It is hereby notified for public information that it has been adopted under resolution No. 05/01  moved at the General 
Conference held on 08.09.2022  at Pradeshiya Sabha Kuliyapitiya that all the roads and thoroughfares for which legal action 
had not been filed in a proper  judicial Court before the date specified  or roads and thoroughfares confirmed as the roads and 
thoroughfares that should be owned by Pradeshiya Sabha Kuliyapitiya as per the Decree of a Judicial Court in which a case 
had been filed before the said date and not mentioned in the following schedule from among the roads and thoroughfares 
given in the list of the schedule of the notification published in the Extraordinary Gazette Paper No. 2273/45  and dated 
30.03.2022 according to the resolution No. 05/03 made at the Pradeshiya Sabha Conference held on 13.01.2021, shall be 
confirmed as roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Kuliyapitiya in terms of orders made by the series of 
“Orders on publication of notifications specifying preparation of plans and lists for roads and throughfares maintained by the 
Pradeshiya Sabha within the North Western Province” published by Extraordinary Gazette Paper No. 2238/35 and dated 
30th July 2021 by the Hon.Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the order by Section 24 (1) of Pradeshiya 
Sabha Act No. 15 of 1987. It is further notified that alist of said roads and thoroughfares has been included in the Schedule 
hereto and all the roads and thoroughfares mentioned in that schedule shall be considered as roads and thoroughfares owned 
by the Pradeshiya Sabha Kuliyapitiya under Sub Section (5) of Section 24 of Pradeshiya Sabha Act.
E. M. Wijayasiri Ekanayaka,
Chairman, 
Pradeshiya Sabha, Kuliyapitiya. 
At the Head Office, 
Pradeshiya  Sabha, Kuliyapitiya,
10
th June 2022.

Pradeshiya Sabha Kuliyapitiya Proposes that the roads and thoroughfares for which legal actions had not been filed in a proper Judicial  Court and not mentioned 
in the following schedule from among the roads and thoroughfares given in the list of the schedule of the notification published in the Extraordinary Gazette Paper 
No. No. 2273/45  and dated 30.03.2021 according to the resolution No. 05/03 made at the Pradeshiya Sabha conference held on 13.01.2021, shall be confirmed as 
roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Kuliyapitiya in terms of orders made by the series of “ Orders on publication of notifications specifying 
preparation of plans and lists for roads and thoroughfares maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabha within the North Western Province” published by Extraordinary 
Gazette  Paper No. 2238/3
5 and dated 30th  July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the order by Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya 
Sabha Act No. 15 of 1987,
